Description:
Embark on a journey through Nepal's rich history, tracing its evolution from ancient dynasties to the modern republic. This video explores the early settlements of the Kathmandu Valley, the rise of the Kirata and Licchavi dynasties, the cultural zenith during the Malla period, and the unification under Prithvi Narayan Shah. Discover the impact of the Rana rule, the struggle for democracy, and the eventual establishment of Nepal as a federal democratic republic in 2008. Dive into the profound cultural and religious influences of Hinduism and Buddhism, which have shaped Nepal's unique identity. Perfect for history enthusiasts and those interested in South Asian culture, this video provides an insightful overview of Nepal's storied past.
